BIRTH AND PLANETARY DATA GATHERED SINCE 1949
(Coordonnées natales et planétaires rassemblées depuis 1949)

Serie A: PROFESSIONAL NOTABILITIES (Notabilités professionnelles)
by Michel et Françoise GAUQUELIN

© Laboratoire d'Étude des Relations entre Rythmes Cosmiques et Psychophysiologiques
L.E.R.R.C.P., Paris, 1970 ; C.U.R.A. (http://cura.free.fr), 2001-2002 ; C.U.R.A. 2009

[5th CURA's edition, revised by Patrice Guinard : February 2009]
 

Notice

PRO : Profession
NUM : Number (from 1 to 2027)
COU : Country (F = born in France, I = Italy, G = Germany, B = Belgium, N = Netherlands, S = Switzerland)
DAY : Day of birth
MON : Month of birth
YEA : Year of birth
H : Hour of birth ; Birthtime is converted to standard time, either for zone 0 (= GMT) or -1 (= CET)
MN : Minutes
SEC : Seconds
TZ : Time Zone at the place of birth and date of birth (0 or -1)
LAT : Latitude of Birth place
LON : Longitude of Birth place
COD : Abbreviated Code of Birth place indicating County of birth or the French "Département"
CITY : Name of Birth place
 

Professions

C = sport Champion (vol. 1)
S = Scientist (vol. 2)
M = Military man (vol. 3)
P = Painter (vol. 4)
M = Musician (vol. 4)
A = Actor (vol. 5)
PT = Politician (vol. 5)
W = Writer (vol. 6)
J = Journalist (vol. 6)
 

Index (vol. 6) :

Writers (Écrivains) : n. 1-1352
Journalists (Journalistes) : n. 1353-2027
 

Repartition by countries (vol. 6)

France : 813
Italy : 659
Belgium : 332
Netherlands : 209
Germany : 14
